    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({

<span id="freeTextContainer2546380892848912018"><i>How do you move on when he’s every song you sing?</i><br/><br/>After Laurelyn Prescott walks away from the love of her life, she returns to Nashville to pursue the only dream she has left.   <span id="freeText2546380892848912018" style="display:none"><i>How do you move on when he’s every song you sing?</i><br /><br />After Laurelyn Prescott walks away from the love of her life, she returns to Nashville to pursue the only dream she has left. Determined to find a distraction from the pain of losing Jack Henry, she immerses herself in her music. But with her old life comes old acquaintances and new expectations. When Laurelyn refuses her record producer’s outrageous demands, she finds herself without a career—until an unforeseen opportunity presents itself. From there it’s a rocket ride straight to the top where Laurelyn finds the success she’s always dreamed of. Will it be enough to bring her the happiness she so deserves, or will the absence of Jack Henry leave her wanting more?<br /><br />Jack Henry McLachlan never expected to fall in love with Laurelyn Prescott—but he did. After he foolishly let her slip through his fingers, he spends three months searching for her, but their reunion doesn’t come easy. The woman he finds isn’t the same one who drifted away without a goodbye. No longer an insecure girl on an Australian adventure, this Laurelyn is a successful musician with a promising career. Her dreams are becoming a reality, and Jack is terrified his American girl won’t have a place for him in her new life. With only a month to convince her otherwise, will it be enough time to make her visualize a life beyond the glitz and glamour, a life that includes him?</span>
  <a data-text-id="2546380892848912018" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer2275022784098351061">Well, Beauty From Pain absolutely blew me away and I fell hard for Jack Henry. I was completely desperate to get my hands on the sequel after that cliffhanger. I was fully invested in these two and really needed them to find the happiness that they both deserve together.<br/><br/><br/>This one picks up pretty much where we left them – separated by several thousand miles and the Pacific Ocean. Laurelyn has returned to America and Jack has absolutely no idea how to find her. After a disastrous and eye-opening at</span>
  <span id="freeText2275022784098351061" style="display:none">Well, Beauty From Pain absolutely blew me away and I fell hard for Jack Henry. I was completely desperate to get my hands on the sequel after that cliffhanger. I was fully invested in these two and really needed them to find the happiness that they both deserve together.<br /><br /><br />This one picks up pretty much where we left them – separated by several thousand miles and the Pacific Ocean. Laurelyn has returned to America and Jack has absolutely no idea how to find her. After a disastrous and eye-opening attempt to find number fourteen, Jack hires a private detective to track Laurelyn down. She has attempted to move on with her life despite her incredible sense of loss after walking away from Jack and Australia.<br /><br />I did enjoy that we got a longer story with these two and an ultimately very happy ending after a period of strife but, in retrospect, I think this may have been better told in just one book. I did really enjoy Jack’s POV in this one and hearing how he was feeling about their situation but I just didn’t love this one as much as the first, sadly.<br /><br /><br />Laurelyn was still a great heroine and I still really loved her. She remains open, engaging, rather sad but ultimately hopeful. She’s attempting to move on with her life, finding happiness in her singing and is considering starting a relationship with one of her band members who is more than a little interested in her. I felt deeply her incredible sadness at the loss of the love of her life and worried about her situation with her mother and father and her horrific ex-boyfriend.<br /><br /><br />Jack for me was just not the guy I fell in love with in Beauty From Pain – he seems to be a whole lot less alpha. He’s still very endearing and very sexy but there was just something here that made him seem a bit feeble compared to how I’d seen him before. He comes across as a broken man rather than as an alpha roaring for his mate. Also, Laurelyn and Jack just seemed to be lacking that fizzing connection and amazing chemistry that I’d been so blown away by in the first book. The sex scenes, although still very hot, did rather lack that intensity that I’d enjoyed before. I’m not also sure we got full closure on some of the backstories – Laurelynn’s relationship with her father, what happened to her ex in the end and what about Audrey?<br /><br />But still, I believe that they got their Happy Ever After that they truly deserve and there’s a beautiful epilogue and there’s still a lot to enjoy in this one. If you loved Beauty From Pain, and so many of us did, this is a must-read to get that sense of completion that we all crave.<br /><br /><br />3.5 stars<br /><br /><i>For more reviews, please visit <a href="http://sinfullysexybooks.blogspot.co.uk/" rel="nofollow noopener">Sinfully Sexy Book Reviews</a> or visit us on <a href="https://www.facebook.com/sinfullysexybookreviews" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a>.</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="2275022784098351061" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer612483624" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer3480991076770557136"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421153i/836320._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>3 SURRENDER STARS.<br/><br/>'Beauty from surrender' picks right up from where we were left hanging with the mother of all cliff hangers in 'beauty from pain'. Yes, for months we have been waiting for answers and they are finally here. The author combines gut wrenching anticipation, and true love yearning in this much anticipated follow up. <br/><br/>Meet the characters ...<br/>Laurelyn Prescott is still as loveable as ever. Feisty, talented but broken over her separation, we are shown the survivor side of our heroine. L</span>
  <span id="freeText3480991076770557136" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421153i/836320._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>3 SURRENDER STARS.<br><br>'Beauty from surrender' picks right up from where we were left hanging with the mother of all cliff hangers in 'beauty from pain'. Yes, for months we have been waiting for answers and they are finally here. The author combines gut wrenching anticipation, and true love yearning in this much anticipated follow up. <br><br>Meet the characters ...<br>Laurelyn Prescott is still as loveable as ever. Feisty, talented but broken over her separation, we are shown the survivor side of our heroine. Laurelyn absolutely won me over in this novel and as I said in my previous review this female lead ticks all the boxes and is easy to fall for.<br><br>Jack Henry McLachlan <br>If I felt indifferent to this character in 'beauty from pain' then I've gone the whole 180 I completely fell for Jack Henry. He shows backbone and I can hardly ever resist a mysterious caveman type, and he fits the bill perfectly for that genre of book husbands.<br><br>What's it all about?<br>A jumble of reunions, questions answered, love finding its way, dreams captured ~ Jack and Laurelyn have faced more than their fair share of misunderstandings and unsaid conversations. We find this couple both heart broken and lost ~ worlds apart from each other. There are obstacles to climb, apologises to be made and a whole host of moving forward before this duo can find their own happily ever after. What you can expect in this story is the journey of hope, of finding what they both want and the possibility of that not coming to pass.<br><br>What I liked ..<br>The chemistry, the development of characters and relationships. The slow build up of will they? Won't they? There's no denying that Geogia Cates captured an audience with beauty from pain and I believe she will be doing it again with the conclusion to Laurelyn and Jack Henry's story.<br><br>What Didn't quite work ...<br>There are some similarities between this series and others of this genre, but that's not a huge minus in my reading experience, it just had a predictability factor that made it an easy ride and at times a little boring. The book was well written and it had the 'nice' factor, rather than the 'wow' factor, so i didn't feel wrapped up in the relationship between the duo and Unfortunately some of the more intimate scenes had a major cringe factor for me, two words - DYSON VACUUM. There is no denying that I enjoyed this novel, but there was something missing for me, and sadly I found myself skim reading towards the end. I would recommend that readers check out other reviews as I'm in a minority with my three stars.<br><br>If like me, your a fan of romance, intrigue, chemistry and plenty of between the sheets action add into the mix likeable characters then I'm pretty much convinced this will tick your must read boxes. sadly for me this time it didn't work out as a 5 star series.<br><br>3 stars.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3480991076770557136" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer524295024" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer4985650318052826496"><b>4.5 Ah-mazing Jacktastick Stars!!! :D </b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506207293i/23997218.jpg' width='400' height='270' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><i>Beauty from Surrender</i> takes place right where <i>Beauty from Pain</i> left off. If you haven’t read <i>Beauty from Pain</i> I highly recommend it! It left me shocked, and a bit distraught. Just a quick summary: We have Jack Henry and Laurelyn-<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506207293i/23997216.jpg' width='400' height='320' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506207293i/23997217.jpg' width='351' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>After a ‘3 month arrangement’ while Laurelyn is in Australia, they fall in love with one another. Well, Laruelyn admits to loving Jack, but the truth is Jack Henry is just not in a place to admit his feelings. So Laurelyn takes of</span>
  <span id="freeText4985650318052826496" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Ah-mazing Jacktastick Stars!!! :D </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506207293i/23997218.jpg" width="400" height="270" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><i>Beauty from Surrender</i> takes place right where <i>Beauty from Pain</i> left off. If you haven’t read <i>Beauty from Pain</i> I highly recommend it! It left me shocked, and a bit distraught. Just a quick summary: We have Jack Henry and Laurelyn-<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506207293i/23997216.jpg" width="400" height="320" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506207293i/23997217.jpg" width="351" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>After a ‘3 month arrangement’ while Laurelyn is in Australia, they fall in love with one another. Well, Laruelyn admits to loving Jack, but the truth is Jack Henry is just not in a place to admit his feelings. So Laurelyn takes off. Jack doesn’t know her full name, so he is having a hard time finding her, but he has to find her. He has never felt this way about anyone before and he’s not sure how he let her go. They both miss each other terribly. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506207514i/23997262.jpg" width="400" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Jack Henry hires someone to go to the States and search for Laurelyn. Laurelyn is just as miserable as he is, but she has to start moving on with her life and her career. She finally gets a break, and joins a band. She is very talented and starting to do well in the industry. She has a famous father who has just entered her life, but she doesn’t want anyone to know. She wants to succeed or fail on her own merit. Then we have the creeper known as Blake who is back in the picture- ugh! Anyway, she starts touring with a couple of guys in an established band and she is doing really well. It gets easier with time, but she still can’t move on from Jack Henry. Can you ever move on from a love like that? <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506207514i/23997263.jpg" width="320" height="420" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Its been months and Jack Henry has followed lead after lead trying to find Laurelyn. He is pretty she he as tracked her down this time. He takes a month off work to go to the States and see her. He gets to Texas (where she happens to be touring at the time) and sees her onstage. Time stops. He knows he will never be able to live another day without her in his life. Their reuniting is emotional. Jack Henry lets his romantic side out in this book. Be ready to swoon for him! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506207514i/23997264.jpg" width="340" height="523" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>The sex scenes between Jack Henry and Laurelyn were just as smokin’ hot! Love me some Jack Henry and his dirty talk! And stripping. I can’t forget the stripping! wow! <br><br>Besides the whole Blake snafu, and some drama with Laurelyn’s parents, things are going great between the two. Thats until its time for Jack Henry to go back to Australia. He has taken as much time as he can. There are huge decisions to be made. Does Laurelyn stay in the states and persue her music career she has worked so hard for? Or does she go back to Australia to start a life with Jack Henry- a real life where they can be together always? I would personally say thats a no-brainer (I would go with you, Jack Henry- no questions asked!) but it’s difficult for Laurelyn to choose. Jack doesn’t want to make her pick him, he doesn’t want her to regret never living her dreams, so he goes back and patiently waits for her decision. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506207640i/23997272.jpg" width="450" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I’m going to stop right there- I don’t want the ending spoiled, but the ending made me a very happy girl! Jack Henry and Laurelyn are a favorite couple of mine. I love them both. This sequel had a lot to live up to. I absolutely loved the first book... so the big question about book 2: Did I love it??? In the words of Jack Henry- <b>Abso-fucking-lutely </b>, maybe not quite as much as the first, but it was still an excellent read! Jack and Laurelyn were mostly on solid ground after they reunited, but they still had struggles with trying to make it work. I’m just going to say how much I love Jack Henry’s mom and brother! Ah it was great catching up with the two of them. I was happy with how it ended, but I think the idea of a 3rd book in the series or a novella would be great. I would like to see how life is for the two of them <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[After the wedding, and maybe making a baby like Jack Henry seems to want so bad <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506207640i/23997273.jpg" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  </blockquote>
</a><br/><b>The Beauty Series is the whirlwind romance</b> of Australia’s most eligible</span>
  <span id="freeText1551817594786110748" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/CatesBeautyfromsurrender2TitlebySueBee_zpsea07e2be.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425222i/848403.jpg" alt=" photo CatesBeautyfromsurrender2TitlebySueBee_zpsea07e2be.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIF%20Sexy%20embrace/dance1bySB_zps40535f82.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1391382440ra/8379772.gif" alt=" photo dance1bySB_zps40535f82.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>★★★★ 1/2! Beauty From Surrender, book 2 of 3. The conclusion of Aussie alpha multimillionaire extraordinaire Jack Henry spellbinding romance of American girl, Laurelyn. A captivating, sexy and memorable read!</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“I want to f~ck on the bonnet, but it might be a little warm for that bum of yours.” He pops his button and unzips. “So I'm gonna f~ck you on the boot and save the bonnet for another time.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><b>The Beauty Series is the whirlwind romance</b> of Australia’s most eligible bachelor, handsome, controlling, elusive, oh so sexy, multi-millionaire <b>Jack Henry McLachlan</b> and his American girl, aspiring country-singer with daddy-issues, <b>Laurelyn Paige Prescott</b>. In their story you will want for nothing; there will be intrigue and villains, sex and seduction. But also personal reflection and growth in the friendship that ensues and the romance that unfolds. <br><br><u>Books in The Beauty Series should be read in order:</u><br><b>Book 1: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/489243243" rel="nofollow noopener">Beauty From Pain</a><br>Book 2: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/640286019" rel="nofollow noopener">Beauty From Surrender</a><br>Book 3: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/636637297" rel="nofollow noopener">Beauty From Love</a></b><br><br><b>Beauty From Surrender (book 2) follows Jack Henry and Laurelyn in the aftermath of book 1’s shocking ending.</b> Both are trying to come to terms with their situation. How will they be able to sort out their feelings and find their way back to each other? Enjoy a slow and long build-up of sexual tension and suspense; Confusion, set-backs, jealousy and stress mars them at every turn of their against-all-odd romance spanning the globe! It is going to take much more than sheer will to bring them back and keep them together. I will say no more I want you to enjoy their story for yourself!<br><br>The Beauty Series is an all-consuming very enjoyable read. Please note that even though a third book has been announced, <b>book 2 is very much the conclusion and the long-sought <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[happily-after <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> ending of their story.</b> Book 3 has been described more as an extended epilogue. <b>My wish would be for book 3 to provide lots of glimpses into Jack Henry’s and Laurelyn’s future.</b><br><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/CatesBeauty1-2HerobySueBee_zpsabcabd69.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402591i/782615.jpg" alt=" photo CatesBeauty1-2HerobySueBee_zpsabcabd69.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I was my absolute pleasure and joy to watch the calculated, bossy and non-committal <b>Jack Henry in his fall into “whopped”</b>. As the story unfolds we will learn and better understand his background including past experiences with women. This is his journey of learning to trust, give up control and opening himself up.<br><br>Six words to describe <b>Jack Henry: Larger-than-life, assertive, controlling, caring, observant, captivating.</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“Abso-fucking-lutely.” *** “Fan-fucking-tastic.”<br><br><br>“I put my hand on the crotch of my pants. “There's only one pole that counts and I've got it right here.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/CatesBeauty1-2HeroinebySueBee_zpsce943c1e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402591i/782616.jpg" alt=" photo CatesBeauty1-2HeroinebySueBee_zpsce943c1e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>A combination of young and fresh yet wise beyond her years, <b>Laurelyn</b> is a wonderful heroine and exactly what Jack Henry needs. She will also go through a transformation; maturing working through some of her issues and searching for her footing in life.<br><br>Five words to describe <b>Laurelyn: Playful, easygoing, charismatic, wise and talented.</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“He is always the song I sing.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><b> Spellbinding story-telling! An all-consuming romance! Scorching hot sex scenes! Well developed and charismatic characters!</b> I very much enjoyed Jack Henry’s and Laurelyn’s journey. Thanks Ms. Cates!<br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“Everything I've been, I am, or will ever be, I surrender it all to you.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br>***<br>Hero rating: 5 stars <br>Heroine rating: 4.5 stars<br>Sex scenes rating: 5 stars<br>Sex scenes frequency: 5 stars<br>Storyline concept rating: 4 stars<br>Storytelling skills rating: 4.5 stars<br>Story ending rating: 4 stars<br>Book editing rating (5 = no edits spotted): 5 stars<br>************************************************<br><b>Overall rating: 4.5 stars<br><br>Would I recommend this series: Yes.<br>Would I re-read this series: Maybe later.<br>Would I read future books by this author: Yes.</b><br><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIF%20Sexy%20embrace/belly2bysb_zps7ac37782.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

              <span id="reviewTextContainer810784201" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer6468154327814070288"> <b>5 Amazing Stars</b>	<br/><br/>This second book starts immediately after the end of the first. Laurelyn is arriving at US, running away from Australia without leaving any form of contact, and Jack is coming home early, ready to tell her what he feels just to find her gone without a goodbye. <br/>He tries to forget her but he soon realizes that he can’t so he hires a private investigator to find her in the US. Since he only knows her first name is not an easy job and is a task that will take three months. <br/>And a lot</span>
  <span id="freeText6468154327814070288" style="display:none"> <b>5 Amazing Stars</b>	<br><br>This second book starts immediately after the end of the first. Laurelyn is arriving at US, running away from Australia without leaving any form of contact, and Jack is coming home early, ready to tell her what he feels just to find her gone without a goodbye. <br>He tries to forget her but he soon realizes that he can’t so he hires a private investigator to find her in the US. Since he only knows her first name is not an easy job and is a task that will take three months. <br>And a lot can change in that time. <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388968742i/7964634._SY540_.png" width="300" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> alt="description"/&gt;<br><br>Three months after, even not moving on from Jack, Laurelyn’s life changed a lot. Starting to make a name in the music world she is getting ready to go on tour and her future is starting in US. <br>So when Jack finally reaches her and they find each other again, can she choose between her future in music and her future with the man she fell in love? <br>And after all that time and with an ocean and a sinful past between them, do they really stand a chance? <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388968743i/7964635.jpg" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I loved this book. Liked it way more than the first probably because it was sweeter and more honest. There was no fake names, no hiding secrets (well, almost any secrets) and they were just trying to have a second chance at their love. <br>The amount of drama on this book was just perfect and I wouldn’t have asked for a better sequel. I can’t wait to read the third! ;) <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388683472i/7901653.jpg" width="350" height="170" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <b>Rating: </b> 5 stars. <br> <b>Storyline: </b> Slightly predictable but totally enjoyable. The drama/romance/ sweetness/steam ratio was perfect. <br> <b>Writing Style: </b> Completely addictive. First person and dual POV. <br> <b>Character Development: </b> Amazing characters. Both of them feel extremely real and their connection is amazing. Neither of them annoyed me (much) which is always good thing. 	<br> <b>Steam: </b> Pretty hot! <br> <b>HEA: </b>	<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_614462384" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/614462384" />
    <a title="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr"><img alt="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1465384674p2/9080319.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/614462384?book_show_action=true">May 13, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" href="/user/show/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr">Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer614462384" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1108396134076698156">4.5 <b>Jack Henry swoon-worthy stars!</b><br/><br/>After that cliffy ending to Beauty From Pain, I couldn't wait to dive into this one. This book starts off right after Laurelyn moves back to the States. She doesn't say goodbye to Jack Henry...she just can't bear to see him say goodbye. This first part was a bit frustrating for me as it takes a while for him to find her. I was under the impression with the amount of money at his disposal, this would not be that difficult. But anyways...... The pacing of the firs</span>
  <span id="freeText1108396134076698156" style="display:none">4.5 <b>Jack Henry swoon-worthy stars!</b><br><br>After that cliffy ending to Beauty From Pain, I couldn't wait to dive into this one. This book starts off right after Laurelyn moves back to the States. She doesn't say goodbye to Jack Henry...she just can't bear to see him say goodbye. This first part was a bit frustrating for me as it takes a while for him to find her. I was under the impression with the amount of money at his disposal, this would not be that difficult. But anyways...... The pacing of the first half is nice and slow much like the first book. Then the second half speeds along more quickly...a week later, <br>two weeks later.... Sometimes that felt a bit rushed to me but it wasn't confusing or distracting.<br><br>We still get the alternating POV of both Laurelyn and Jack Henry but not quite as back and forth in frequency as the first book. It flowed nicely though. I liked getting into each of their heads. Jack Henry has to find Laurelyn and when he does he prays she still loves him and will commit to a future with him...a future in Australia. But she has a budding music career. Will she give it all up to move Down Under? Laurelyn has always counted on herself alone to succeed in this world. It's a huge risk to give up all her hard work for a guy who, a few months ago, only had short term, no-strings-attached agreements. How can someone possibly change so much?<br><br>Okay, I seriously think Jack Henry is the shizzle. We fell in love with him in BFP as being the rich, self protective hotness on a stick.<br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Used%20in%20review/5b3fd0cd6a3873f4e1052141e4c773cf_zps3bdd1577.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421443i/837171._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 5b3fd0cd6a3873f4e1052141e4c773cf_zps3bdd1577.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br> But in this book, all bets are off and he will do just about anything in the name of love. Things that terrified him in BFP he finds himself dreaming of having someday soon.....with Laurelyn. He loves Laurelyn and will do anything to get her to commit to him forever. No more women...she's it for him. The sexual chemistry between these two is off the hook. He's clearly a god in bed! Seven hours of godliness. Everything about him is endearing.... Laurelyn is a fairly strong heroine. To walk away like she did may look weak but it was more self preservation. She did a few things in this book that annoyed me- games she played with Jack Henry but she by far is a very UN-annoying heroine. We get so many weak, spineless ones in books of late and that she is not. I guess she is only 23 which, to me, is still very young for the decisions she had to face....<br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Used%20in%20review/bc6aa7e662a9850a076df8558fb7e975_zpsba44da3e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421443i/837172._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo bc6aa7e662a9850a076df8558fb7e975_zpsba44da3e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>I loved the secondary characters! Jack's mom Margaret is a HOOT! I couldn't resist falling in love with her. His brother Evan was also a stronger character in this book. I enjoyed the antics between these two. The family relationship between all of them was just believable.... Relatable. <br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Used%20in%20review/d698db64a640eeedbe514f8535d2c2e5_zpsbf5e1aae.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421443i/837173._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo d698db64a640eeedbe514f8535d2c2e5_zpsbf5e1aae.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Used%20in%20review/2477a1e5cbf6abc8708a07b874ae4766_zps3b724ed1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408076i/797947._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 2477a1e5cbf6abc8708a07b874ae4766_zps3b724ed1.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The book ends in the HEA we hoped for thru both books. The author notes she will likely write a third book <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[post marriage <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> but has left it in a good spot in case readers want to stop here. I guess there's some potential issues still lurking in the shadows that could add some more angst to their story but I'm totally good with the book as she's left it.<br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Used%20in%20review/a9898a8658b6fbfab978c4bae6972dcb_zpsd262f010.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421443i/837174._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo a9898a8658b6fbfab978c4bae6972dcb_zpsd262f010.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> </["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/544261035?book_show_action=true">Feb 23, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessica&#39;s Book Review" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessica&#39;s Book Review" href="/user/show/9816167-jessica-s-book-review">Jessica&#39;s Book Review</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer544261035" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10880839543727009707"><a href='http://jessicasbookreview.blogspot.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Read more reviews on my blog</a> | <a href='https://www.facebook.com/JessicasBookReview' rel='nofollow noopener'>Like me on Facebook</a><br/><br/><br/>Ladies, prepare to have Jack Henry melt your panties off! If it is even possible I am more in love with him now then I was before! He is simply amazing and such a wonderful man in Beauty From Surrender. Everything I loved about him in Beauty From Pain just multiplies in BFS and he is seriously the perfect guy. He is caring, LOVING, mature, sexy, rich, he is just <b>EVERYTHING</b> that is perfection. He might just be my ALL TIME book boyfriend, yep, that</span>
  <span id="freeText10880839543727009707" style="display:none"><a href="http://jessicasbookreview.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Read more reviews on my blog</a> | <a href="https://www.facebook.com/JessicasBookReview" rel="nofollow noopener">Like me on Facebook</a><br><br><br>Ladies, prepare to have Jack Henry melt your panties off! If it is even possible I am more in love with him now then I was before! He is simply amazing and such a wonderful man in Beauty From Surrender. Everything I loved about him in Beauty From Pain just multiplies in BFS and he is seriously the perfect guy. He is caring, LOVING, mature, sexy, rich, he is just <b>EVERYTHING</b> that is perfection. He might just be my ALL TIME book boyfriend, yep, that is right! <b>ALL TIME</b>.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410886i/806294._SX540_.jpg" width="350" height="238" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410886i/806295._SY540_.jpg" width="315" height="326" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Beauty From Surrender picks up right where Beauty From Pain leaves off. Those who have read BFP were given the first two chapters of BFS and know what a crazy cliff hanger/wait this has been. I was one of those bloggers stalking Amazon waiting for the moment it is released and devoured the book within hours! I read the entire book all in one night. I just LOVED IT! If you follow my blog or Facebook you know I have said many times the Beauty Series by Georgia Cates is my one of my favorites of all time, beating books such as Fifty Shades of Grey that is how in love I am with this series.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410886i/806296._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What I loved most about BFS is it still had the same feel BFP had. There are decisions to be made, feelings to be expressed, all with a time clock clicking over the heads of Laurelyn &amp; Jack. Though the story was different it still had that magical feel BFP had. I also loved that it was not cheesy or unrealistic love. They may have expressed their feelings but it wasn’t over the top and Jack &amp; Laurelyn were still themselves just like the last book and did not change.<br><br>This time around Laurelyn has big choices to make involving her future. She is in the driver’s seat of their relationship controlling Jack and her future together. I just adore Laurelyn too! I love her sarcastic personality and her tough wit; she is my favorite book heroine. Jack Henry’s mother also was a star in this book. Can his family be any better? Laurelyn is a lucky girl!<br><br>The book does leave off with a possibility for a third book in the series sometime down the road. I really hope there is one because there are a few things left to be unsolved and of course I must know how Jack Henry &amp; Laurelyn are doing. I was seriously swooning over the lines Jack said to Laurelyn… gosh this man is my god… like seriously!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410886i/806297._SY540_.png" width="350" height="525" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The first half of the book is slow, which I LOVED! Sometimes I felt BFP went too fast so this was a nice change and more drawn out. The scene of Jack &amp; Laurelyn seeing each other again for the first time is epic. I am glad it was played out well &amp; slow; made it even better for us readers. About half way through the book, the book picks up speed and quickly goes through weeks and months. I did miss the slow speed of the book from the beginning, even the ending was a bit too fast for me.<br><br>I love this book and though it might not be as <i>amazing</i> as the first book in the series Beauty From Pain it is still really great! There are still a few questions left unanswered for me… mainly where certain characters went. I hope this is leading up to a third book. Georgia has said she plans to write a novel or novella for Jack &amp; Laurelyn’s story but not for awhile, I want it SOON!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410886i/806298._SX540_.png" width="350" height="153" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410886i/806299._SX540_.png" width="370" height="145" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Beauty From Surrender is a great second book for the series. I am always worried about second books but this did not disappoint! Jack Henry alone makes it perfect but the story and characters keep getting better as well.<br><br>I give Beauty From Surrender (Beauty #2) 4 Stars.</span>
  <a data-text-id="10880839543727009707" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

You don't need me to tell you how you'll know if she's the one." "My heart's not telling me anything.   <span id="freeText10296044099228193161" style="display:none"><b>3 Mr. McLachlan and the Paths we choose in Life Stars<br><br><i>"Nothing speaks louder than your heart. Listen to what it's telling you. You don't need me to tell you how you'll know if she's the one." "My heart's not telling me anything. It's screaming in desperation to find her and tell her how much I love her."</i></b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408348i/798771.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Jack and Laurelyn</b>, refused their hearts' demands and turned their backs on love. Laurelyn returned to America trying to pick up the pieces of her broken heart and left Jack alone to realise what he had and lost. What he let to walk away and the love he had in his grasp and he allowed to slip through his fingers.<br><br><b>
  <i>He will always be every song I sing.</i>
</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>♪♫I made the decision to walk away <br>And now there's so much distance between you and me. <br>Now you're so far away, so very far away. <br>Will you always remain out of my reach? <br>It's easy to lie myself <br>but I fear my stupid heart will never be free.♪♫</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Now, while Laurelyn faces her parents and tries to build the career that she always dreamed, Jack will desperately look for her and finally admit his feelings. Will they be enough? Will they have a chance to a future together? And more, will they choose to sacrifice their hopes and dreams for happiness?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408348i/798772.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Passionate and exciting this is a nice conclusion to Jack and Laurelyn's story about love and surrender. Extremely hot, this couple is making the pages sizzle with their chemistry and your heart sigh with their funny banter.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380408348ra/798773.gif" width="400" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But, huge BUT and the reason behind my lower than expected rating.... I feel that the book dragged a wee bit without reason. Predictable and pretty much uneventful, I didn't feel it lived up to all the expectations, built up from the first book.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396644ra/764838.gif" width="400" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Everything was pretty much resolved by 49% and the constant what ifs, angst with no reason and the obvious solution to all the dilemmas, frustrated me and kinda bored me. Additionaly, the almost non-existent secondary character involvement, aside Laurelyn's screw-up parents, deadbeat bastard ex and Jack's delightful mother, didn't help in picking up the pace.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380408348ra/798774.gif" width="352" height="260" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Jack and Laurelyn failed to stand up to the circumstances, face the situation and just plain admit that they can't live without each other!!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380408348ra/798775.gif" width="400" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Don't take all this wrong. This is NOT a bad book. This is actually a great story that yes, leaves you in a really good place. I read the author's note about a possible 3rd book. I don't think it will bring anything more to the story as it is, but maybe by introducing some new blood and interesting twists it will be a great addition. I can say for sure that I will give it a try and we will see.... Well if for nothing else, then at least for Jack's dirty mouth and imagination!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408348i/798776.jpg" width="400" height="266" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer527544261" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10966943273609570022">meh.<br/><br/>This is another for the "everyone loves it but me" shelf. Once again, I just couldn't really connect with Jack or Laurelyn. There were some things I really enjoyed -some very sweet lines, and sexy scenes, but for most of the book it felt like a lot of sex, and ALMOST drama leading up to an inevitable, and unexciting conclusion.<br/><br/>I did appreciate that the author didn't go down (or at least not very far down) some of the drama roads she set up. There were a few that I was SURE where going to hap</span>
  <span id="freeText10966943273609570022" style="display:none">meh.<br /><br />This is another for the "everyone loves it but me" shelf. Once again, I just couldn't really connect with Jack or Laurelyn. There were some things I really enjoyed -some very sweet lines, and sexy scenes, but for most of the book it felt like a lot of sex, and ALMOST drama leading up to an inevitable, and unexciting conclusion.<br /><br />I did appreciate that the author didn't go down (or at least not very far down) some of the drama roads she set up. There were a few that I was SURE where going to happen, that just fizzled. However, the one she DID choose, I just felt too lukewarm. It was an issue, but not a BIG issue, so the drama didn't feel like it had any real urgency - it just fell kind of flat.<br /><br />I think if you loved the first book, you'll enjoy seeing the conclusion of Jack and Laurely's story. If, like me, you didn't love book one, I don't think this will convert you. </span>
  <a data-text-id="10966943273609570022" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_629209796" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/629209796" />
    <a title="Kim  *Mo Chridhe*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9909997-kim-mo-chridhe"><img alt="Kim  *Mo Chridhe*" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1431962494p2/9909997.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/629209796?book_show_action=true">May 31, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kim  *Mo Chridhe*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kim  *Mo Chridhe*" href="/user/show/9909997-kim-mo-chridhe">Kim  *Mo Chridhe*</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9909997-kim-mo-chridhe?shelf=gag-me-with-a-spoon">gag-me-with-a-spoon</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer629209796" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16942574683267288929">Thank God that's over.<br/><br/><b>WARNING!!!! MAJOR SPOILERS AHEAD!!!!</b><br/><br/><br/><br/><br/><br/>I <b>did not</b> see the point of this book. If Ms. Cates wanted to give Jack and Laurelyn their HEA I think an epilogue would've sufficed. My main problem with this book is that THE MAIN PROBLEM was resolved so early in the story that it just went downhill from there. And don't even argue that the main conflict in this book was Jack vs. Laurelyn's career. It wasn't. Ever since <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17156015.Beauty_From_Pain__Beauty___1_' title='Beauty From Pain (Beauty, #1) by Georgia Cates' rel='nofollow noopener'>Beauty From Pain</a>, I never felt Laurelyn's devotion to music as a car</span>
  <span id="freeText16942574683267288929" style="display:none">Thank God that's over.<br /><br /><b>WARNING!!!! MAJOR SPOILERS AHEAD!!!!</b><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br />I <b>did not</b> see the point of this book. If Ms. Cates wanted to give Jack and Laurelyn their HEA I think an epilogue would've sufficed. My main problem with this book is that THE MAIN PROBLEM was resolved so early in the story that it just went downhill from there. And don't even argue that the main conflict in this book was Jack vs. Laurelyn's career. It wasn't. Ever since <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17156015.Beauty_From_Pain__Beauty___1_" title="Beauty From Pain (Beauty, #1) by Georgia Cates" rel="nofollow noopener">Beauty From Pain</a>, I never felt Laurelyn's devotion to music as a career. For me, her being a singer/musician just came across as trivial instead of being an all-encompassing part of her character. There was no competition there. <br /><br />Another beef I have with this book was the writing. Several scenes and dialogues sounded so unnatural and unconvincing! For instance, I thought Margaret assaulting her son with her handbag was OTT and corny. Oh, you know what else is corny? These:<br /><br /><blockquote><b><i>"When I fell before, you didn't catch me."</i><br /><br />She puts my face back on my chest and I'm grateful because I don't want her looking into the windows of my soul.</b> (WHO CALLS THEIR EYES, "WINDOWS OF MY SOUL?!" I think this only works for poetic declarations of love by lonely, old men.)<br /><br /><b><i>"I'm close to blasting my swimmers into your cockpit."</i></b> (I'm embarrassed for you, Jack)</blockquote><br /><br />The writing did <b>nothing</b> for me. The flow of the story was choppy and disjointed. I was talking to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/10366969-chel" rel="nofollow noopener">CHEL</a> about the characters and we both found it odd that some of them just vanished without a fluid exit. I feel as though they were included in the story because, I don't know, Jack and Laurelyn needed enemies. But as soon as they're done with their antagonist roles then they're gone. Poof! Like that woman who confronted Laurelyn in the washroom (bathroom) and thought that it was appropriate to "warn" her of Jack's propositioning ways. And then as soon as Laurelyn felt woozy she's all, "oh, it's my fault because I told her what you did blah blah blah." And we never really found out who the person behind the vineyard casualties were, did we? Jack assumed it was Audrey but I don't remember it being confirmed. I liked <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user_status/show/28264772" rel="nofollow noopener">my theory</a> better. Just sayin'. <br /><br />I don't know. Unlike <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17156015.Beauty_From_Pain__Beauty___1_" title="Beauty From Pain (Beauty, #1) by Georgia Cates" rel="nofollow noopener">Beauty From Pain</a>, everything just felt convenient here. Addison moving to Australia so Laurelyn takes over her audition and automatically blows everyone's minds away, Addison <i>moving to Australia</i>, Laurelyn's mom doing a complete 180 and showing up at the wedding after being so vocally against the whole thing, Laurelyn leaving the band without any problems. Everyone was so easily agreeable and accepting that it didn't seem believable.<br /><br />I guess what stopped me from completely hating this book was the fact Jack and Laurelyn never did anything extremely stupid to anger me. They didn't do anything that wowed me either, which is sad, because I really loved them in the first book. I just wished that Ms. Cates was able to take this further in terms of plot and character development because honestly, this was weak and mediocre. </span>
  <a data-text-id="16942574683267288929" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Christie«SHBBblogger»" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6650940-christie-shbbblogger"><img alt="Christie«SHBBblogger»" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1537729030p2/6650940.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/524468771?book_show_action=true">Feb 02, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christie«SHBBblogger»" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christie«SHBBblogger»" href="/user/show/6650940-christie-shbbblogger">Christie«SHBBblogger»</a>

        rated it

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer524468771" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12059683945798321267">It's finally happened:<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407850i/797124.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>All right, I can't believe I am about to say this, but....there was a bit too much down 'n dirty going on and not enough STORY. Don't get me wrong, I enjoy the heck out of the erotic parts of a good book, but it seemed like this was JUST sex and the rest kind of filler. <br/><br/>Laurelyn and Jack Henry are one of my favorite book couples and I absolutely loved their story in Beauty from pain. The plot was so dazzling and enthralling while the dynamic between the two of them was witt</span>
  <span id="freeText12059683945798321267" style="display:none">It's finally happened:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407850i/797124.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>All right, I can't believe I am about to say this, but....there was a bit too much down 'n dirty going on and not enough STORY. Don't get me wrong, I enjoy the heck out of the erotic parts of a good book, but it seemed like this was JUST sex and the rest kind of filler. <br><br>Laurelyn and Jack Henry are one of my favorite book couples and I absolutely loved their story in Beauty from pain. The plot was so dazzling and enthralling while the dynamic between the two of them was witty, smart and made you beg for more of their perfect connection. In this book, this is pretty much how it goes...<br><br>Reunion around 15%<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407850i/797125.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Lots and lots of reunion Nookie while in denial that they live in different countries.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380407850ra/797126.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Psycho ex drama<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380407850ra/797127.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Seperation filled with angst and some phone nookie<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/516973.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407850i/797128.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Second reunion and....yup more reunion nookie.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380407850ra/797129.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Another psycho kinda-ex drama and kinda-seperation<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380407850ra/797130.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407850i/797131.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380824956i/3126212.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Happily ever after<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407850i/797132.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There are a couple more story plot lines like Laurelyn's parents and another guy in love with her. None of them are really fully fleshed out and I would've like to have seen some more depth into either one of these to make to story a bit more well rounded. I still gave it 3 stars because of how much I adore this couple, the sex WAS hot and sexy, and their bantering was still amazingly funny and adorable. Overall, I enjoyed this book but it fell a little short of book one's magnificence.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12059683945798321267" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/634042330" />
    <a title="* Meli Mel *" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10905711-meli-mel"><img alt="* Meli Mel *" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577750127p2/10905711.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/634042330?book_show_action=true">Jun 05, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="* Meli Mel *" class="user" itemprop="url" name="* Meli Mel *" href="/user/show/10905711-meli-mel">* Meli Mel *</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=fav-book-boyfriend">fav-book-boyfriend</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer634042330" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5028606315180781748"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420823i/835273.jpg' width='125' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>♥♥♥ 3 Stars ♥♥♥</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380424296i/845798._SY540_.jpg' height='500' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br/><br/>"You don't always know the true worth of a women's love until it becomes a memory."<br/>-- Evan McLachlan<br/><br/>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg' width='405' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>Beauty from Surrender</i> picks up where it left off. Laurelyn has returned to Nashville in order to sort out her career. Jack Henry is distraught about not having the chance to tell Laurelyn how he feels. With no way to communicate with her, he thinks he will never see or</span>
  <span id="freeText5028606315180781748" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420823i/835273.jpg" width="125" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>♥♥♥ 3 Stars ♥♥♥</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380424296i/845798._SY540_.jpg" height="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"You don't always know the true worth of a women's love until it becomes a memory."<br>-- Evan McLachlan<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Beauty from Surrender</i> picks up where it left off. Laurelyn has returned to Nashville in order to sort out her career. Jack Henry is distraught about not having the chance to tell Laurelyn how he feels. With no way to communicate with her, he thinks he will never see or hear from her again. The only way he thinks he will be able to get over her, is to look for number fourteen. This only ends up making him realize that he can't be with another woman, he needs to find Laurelyn. Unfortunately, this proves to be a lot more difficult than he anticipated. When, he finally does find her, he doesn't know if she will choose him, or the rising musical career that she has made for herself while they were apart. Jack Henry isn't willing to lose her again, so he must come up with a way to prove to her that he is what she needs.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I <b>really</b> liked the first installment of this story. I <b>absolutely</b> loved Jack Henry and all of the other characters. I'm <b>sad</b> to say that this one <b>didn't</b> really pull through for <b>me</b>.<br><br>It started out great. I was <b>highly</b> anticipating this one after how the first one <b>ended</b>. The separation has been <b>hell</b> for both of them. Time is slowly going on and Laurelyn has decided <b>maybe</b> it's time to move on. After her ex and producer <b>threatens</b> to end her career if she doesn't be with him, she <b>leaves</b> to join a band and is finding <b>success</b> with them. The lead singer, seems to be having <b>feelings</b> for her. So she thinks it might be time to give him a <b>chance</b>, maybe. At this point, I could <b>not</b> wait for them to be <b>reunited</b>.<br><br>And boy, do they <b>reunite</b>! There were having a <b>non-stop sexathon</b>. I don't mind it if a book has a lot of sex scenes, I think it's <b>great</b>! *don't judge*<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/360560.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I never thought there could be <b>too</b> many sex scenes, crazy right? But there <b>was</b>. I felt like it became <b>too much</b> for me. I <b>desperately</b> wanted <b>more</b> story and <b>less</b> sex, I wasn't enjoying it anymore. It was too exaggerated. I kept thinking <b>how</b> is this possible? How is she even <b>walking</b>?! <br><br>And then came the comparison to a <b>dyson vacuum</b>.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380424296ra/845799.gif" width="350" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Yup, she <b>compared</b> Jack Henry's <b>oral</b> skills to a freaking <b>vacuum</b>. I totally <b>thought</b> that was weird, <b>not</b> sexy. But she kept doing it, <b>repeatedly</b>.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380423734i/844401._SY540_.jpg" height="350" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Moving on, I still <b>LOVE</b> Jack Henry! He was too perfect! He went through all this trouble and <b>didn't</b> give up until he <b>found</b> her. I feel like he was the one who <b>grew</b> the most. He doesn't do <b>commitment</b> or <b>babies</b>, and now he is <b>contemplating</b> it with Laurelyn. I loved his <b>dirty</b> mouth, and the <b>swoony</b> things he would say. <b>How</b> could you resist him?<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"I don't regret you for a second. You're my favorite complication and you always will be. I knew you were the next one the second I laid my eyes on you singing in that club, but you never imagine my surprise when I realized you weren't just the next one -- you were the last one."<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380424296i/845800._SY540_.jpg" height="350" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Well, Laurelyn had trouble saying <b>yes</b> to him. I get that she had a <b>career</b> that's she worked <b>hard</b> for. I <b>didn't</b> think it was <b>fair</b> for her to just <b>give</b> that all up. But, when you see her clearly <b>not</b> enjoying it 100%, I <b>didn't</b> get why she wouldn't just <b>go</b> to Australia. I <b>did</b> like Laurelyn, <b>despite</b> her indecisiveness. She was <b>confident</b> and I really liked that about her. But, there was <b>one</b> moment where I feel she <b>overreacted</b>. <br><br>I <b>loved</b> Jack Henry's family, <b>especially</b> his mom, she was a <b>hoot</b>. I can't say the same for Laurelyn's family. I thought her mom was <b>selfish</b> and her father was <b>no better</b>. He left his wife after their son died <b>for</b> Laurelyn's mom. That must have <b>really</b> sucked for his ex-wife, <b>losing</b> her son and husband. I didn't like that they both kept acting as though <b>nothing</b> had ever happened, like he had <b>never</b> been missing from their lives for <b>twenty-three years</b>.<br><br>I would have liked to know <b>more</b> on what ended up happening with the two <b>psychos</b> of this book, <b>Audrey and Blake</b>. They kind of just <b>disappeared</b> and was never seen or heard from again. I found this to be <b>odd</b>, being how they were such <b>creepy stalkers</b>.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"You kissed my heart awake."<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380424296ra/845801.gif" width="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Overall, I was <b>not</b> wowed by this book, but it was a <b>hot, good</b> read. I <b>am</b> happy, however, that they got a <b>HEA</b>. It took a long time for it but they <b>finally</b> got it. There were moments where I <b>smiled and chuckled</b> at the dialogue between Laurelyn and Jack Henry. Still, besides the whole, <b>'Will they be together or not?'</b>, there wasn't much going on. I really needed something <b>exciting</b> to happen. There were some parts that were so <b>drawn out</b> and some a bit <b>rushed</b>. Like I always say, what might <b>not</b> work for me, might <b>for</b> you. So who knows, you might <b>enjoy</b> this book <b>more</b> than I did.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="5028606315180781748" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_556324761" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/556324761" />
    <a title="Brenna" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12928663-brenna"><img alt="Brenna" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1580475762p2/12928663.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/556324761?book_show_action=true">Mar 09, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Brenna" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Brenna" href="/user/show/12928663-brenna">Brenna</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12928663-brenna?shelf=romantic">romantic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12928663-brenna?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12928663-brenna?shelf=rich-hero">rich-hero</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer556324761" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17542797252324202620"><i>
  <b>"He will always be every song I sing."</b>
</i><br/><br/>I read <i>Beauty From Pain</i> almost two years ago and I absolutely loved it. After doing an audio re-read of it, I decided it was the perfect time to continue on with Jack Henry and Laurelyn’s story. Unfortunately, <i>Beauty From Surrender</i> was just <i>okay</i> for me. <br/><br/>At the end of <i>Beauty From Pain</i>, Laurelyn leaves Australia and Jack Henry without a goodbye, desperately in love with him and thinking her feelings were unrequited. When Jack Henry discovers her gone, he’s</span>
  <span id="freeText17542797252324202620" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>"He will always be every song I sing."</b>
</i><br /><br />I read <i>Beauty From Pain</i> almost two years ago and I absolutely loved it. After doing an audio re-read of it, I decided it was the perfect time to continue on with Jack Henry and Laurelyn’s story. Unfortunately, <i>Beauty From Surrender</i> was just <i>okay</i> for me. <br /><br />At the end of <i>Beauty From Pain</i>, Laurelyn leaves Australia and Jack Henry without a goodbye, desperately in love with him and thinking her feelings were unrequited. When Jack Henry discovers her gone, he’s heartbroken because he never got to tell her his true feelings. Without knowing her real last name and without any way to contact her, he hires someone to track her down. <br /><i>
  <blockquote>“I’m going to do everything in my power to make it up to her because I hate what me without her looks like. I’m going to win her back, and when I do, I’m never letting her go again.”</blockquote>
</i><br />I was surprised by how quickly they are back together and their reunion isn’t drawn out at all. Most of the book is spent with them happy and sexing it up while avoiding figuring out how to move forward. Laurelyn’s music career is just taking off and it’s the worst possible time for her to pick up and move back to Australia with Jack Henry, so that is where the conflict of the book lies. <br /><i>
  <blockquote>Our moments together are always the grains of sand falling through the hourglass. A few months here. Another month there. I’m sick of having time restraints placed on this relationship like we have an expiration date.</blockquote>
</i><br />I enjoyed parts of this book (especially ones with JH's mom), but it seemed almost unneeded. I think I would have preferred if <i>Beauty From Pain</i> had been a bit longer or had an epilogue because this book just didn’t have much meat to it. Thankfully there wasn’t tons of unnecessary drama, just a small thing here and there but that made the whole thing seem kind of drawn out for no reason. I found myself skimming, which I hate, and was practically skipping over sex scenes completely because there were so many. By the way, <i>“ecstasy controller”</i> and <i>“dyson vacuum”</i> were definitely new ones for me, but definitely didn’t help my attention span with the sex scenes or this book.<br /><br />I still have some mad love for Jack Henry, but I felt like he lost some of his spark here. Instead of being the dirty talking, sexy, alpha we met in BFP, he just seemed kind of whipped. I am a fan of their relationship, but I hate when there’s a sequel for no reason and it ends up feeling like a waste. I can’t even imagine what the third one is about, but I’m guessing… <i>babies</i> –since that topic comprised almost half of their conversations during this book. I think I’m going to call it a day and just pretend it ended after BFP and they live happily ever after. <br /><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“Everything I’ve been, I am, or will ever be, I surrender it all to you.” <br />“You’re surrendering your all to me, and I can’t think of anything more beautiful than that.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="17542797252324202620" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>
