<div id="review_556320577" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/556320577" />
    <a title="AJ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3143126-aj"><img alt="AJ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406382884p2/3143126.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/556320577?book_show_action=true">Mar 09, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="AJ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="AJ" href="/user/show/3143126-aj">AJ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=omg-romantic">omg-romantic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=feeeeels">feeeeels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=pb-i-own">pb-i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=romantic">romantic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=billionaire">billionaire</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer556320577" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16027472889990767149">If it is possible to swoon to death, I think Jack Henry may just do it…<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794658i/595237._SX540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Damn! I’ve had to wait a while to write this review, because I was left in a puddle of goo on the floor after finishing the book, and only now, the day after, do I feel capable of constructing sentences. <br/><br/>I absolutely loved <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17156015.Beauty_From_Pain__Beauty___1_' title='Beauty From Pain (Beauty, #1) by Georgia Cates' rel='nofollow noopener'>Beauty From Pain</a>. The story of Jack Henry and Laurelyn completely captivated me, and I have been eagerly awaiting the rest of the story. The book picks up right after the end of that devastating cliffy, wit</span>
  <span id="freeText16027472889990767149" style="display:none">If it is possible to swoon to death, I think Jack Henry may just do it…<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794658i/595237._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Damn! I’ve had to wait a while to write this review, because I was left in a puddle of goo on the floor after finishing the book, and only now, the day after, do I feel capable of constructing sentences. <br><br>I absolutely loved <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17156015.Beauty_From_Pain__Beauty___1_" title="Beauty From Pain (Beauty, #1) by Georgia Cates" rel="nofollow noopener">Beauty From Pain</a>. The story of Jack Henry and Laurelyn completely captivated me, and I have been eagerly awaiting the rest of the story. The book picks up right after the end of that devastating cliffy, with Laurelyn returning to the US, desperately in love with Jack but thinking he doesn’t love her, leaving Jack in Australia, devastated and furious with himself for not telling Laurelyn how he felt while he had the chance. <br><br>Devastated and miserable, Jack Henry is broken. But he realises that Laurelyn is the only woman for him, and is determined to track her down. <br><br><i>“I’m going to do everything in my power to make it up to her because I hate what me without her looks like. I’m going to win her back, and when I do, I‘m never letting go of her again.”</i><br><br>Meanwhile, Laurelyn is just as heartbroken, but she tries to pick up her life, throwing herself back into her singing career. Things don’t go smoothly, but amidst dramas with her producer, and her selfish mother, she manages to find success with an up and coming country band. <br><br>And then life is thrown into a spin for both of them when Jack Henry finds her. OMG, my heart was racing, and I was squeeing like an idiot. Their reunion takes place as you would expect – a small amount of talking before they are all over each other, followed shortly by declarations of love, and that’s just the start of the swoon.<br><br><i> “I love you so much, Laurelyn. I swear I do.”<br>…<br>“It was a mistake to not tell you how I felt. It's haunted me since the day I came home and found you gone. You'll never know how sorry I am for letting you slip through my fingers. But it won't happen again because I'm never letting you go. Ever”</i><br><br>OMG, Jack Henry! He loves his girl passionately, and he embraces those feelings whole heartedly. No longer afraid of what he’s feeling, and letting her know it. And, of course, the two of them together are HOT, HOT, HOTTTT!!! Jack Henry has a filthy mouth, and some blow-your-mind moves - <i>“You’re ordering up some extra dirty with a side of kink today”</i>, but as hot as it is, it’s fairly vanilla, with nothing too disturbing going on. <br><br><i>“A gentleman would have pretended he didn’t see those.”<br>“I think we’ve established that I’m only a gentleman in public – not in the bedroom. But I must tell you that it makes me feel pretty damn spectacular to know that you needed two of those battery-operated boys to replace what I did for you.”</i><br><br>I loved seeing them together in an actual relationship. They are open and honest with their feelings, and say what is on their mind, but they also acknowledge their difficulties, because underneath all of the romance is the fear of the future. Jack’s future is in Australia, Laurelyn’s career is in the US. They both know that they need to be together, but how do they make it happen?<br><br><i>“I hear her soft, sweet voice against my ear and feel her trembling in my arms.<br>“Don’t leave,” she whispers. <br>I feel the tears when they come and I bury my face in her hair. “Don’t let me leave without you.”</i><br><br>But despite their heartfelt pleas *sniff*, neither one of them pressured the other to uproot their lives, respecting each other's careers, and acknowleding the sacrifice that would be required without making any demands. <br><br>Jack Henry and Laurelyn are fantastic together, and the passion and intense connection between them leaps off the page. They experience huge ups and downs on the way to their HEA, but they dynamic between them is fantastic - I was constantly either swooning, laughing or fanning myself. Jack is definitely Alpha, but Laurelyn is a strong heroine, and their relationship is an equal one. They are functional, for the most part, although Laurelyn has a moment of stupid towards the end, and I thought she was way out of line with how she handled the situation, but I was never in any doubt about how the story would end. <br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<i>“Laurelyn, I once asked you to be mine for three months. Now, I’m asking you to be mine forever.” She opens her mouth to speak and I place my fingers to her lips. “But I don’t want your answer right now because you’re not ready to say yes. You still need time to spread your wings and fly. I love you with all my heart and I want you to experience everything this life has to offer you because it won’t wait. But I will. I’ll wait for you as long as it takes, and you can come to me after you ‘ve had enough of this life…when you’re ready to spend forever with me.”<br><br></i>… and then…<i><br><br>“Today I lay at your feet the man I’ve been so I may become the man you need me to be.”</i><br><br>OMG… SWOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOON!!! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Big shout out to Jack Henry’s family, I love them all! They are so funny, and the dynamics between them are brilliant. In particular, Jacks’ discussions with his brother, Evan, had me laughing out loud, and his mother is absolutely sensational.<br><br><i>“I interrupted whatever you were doing?”<br>“Indeed you did.”<br>“Son, if you stopped to answer the phone, then you weren’t doing </i>whatever<i> well enough and you need to get back to her and do it better. Don’t answer the phone next time.”<br>Damn. I just got zinged by my mum.”</i><br><br>The book finishes off with a beautiful HEA, although I would have loved an epilogue. Georgia Cates is hinting at either another novel or novella to finish off Jack Henry and Laurelyn’s story in more detail, and I would love to see that happen. But in the meantime, I am very content with everything exactly as it is.<br><br>4.5 swoontastic stars.<br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="16027472889990767149" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/539472209?book_show_action=true">Feb 18, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads">Jacqueline&#39;s Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=4-star-books">4-star-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer539472209" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7563873288820021934"><br/><a href='http://imgur.com/Pfhxy0l' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410173i/803850._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>4 Stars<br/><br/>WHOA… One word to describe <i>Beauty from Surrender</i> is SEX!!! <br/><br/>Lots and lots of S.E.X!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://imgur.com/tVL8cuU' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380405238ra/789147.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I liked <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/533510730' rel='nofollow noopener'>Beauty from Pain</a>, even with the epic cliffy **shaking head**, so you can see how very excited I was for <i>Beauty from Surrender</i><br/><br/><b>Disclaimer</b> There is no cliffy in <i>Beauty from Surrender</i> and there’s a HEA, but there’s enough of an opening for book 3, which from reading Georgia Cate’s blog, hasn’t been decided if it’s going to be a full novel or novella. <br/><br/>I’ll tell you now… I will read book 3 and I pr</span>
  <span id="freeText7563873288820021934" style="display:none"><br><a href="http://imgur.com/Pfhxy0l" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410173i/803850._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>4 Stars<br><br>WHOA… One word to describe <i>Beauty from Surrender</i> is SEX!!! <br><br>Lots and lots of S.E.X!</b><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/tVL8cuU" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380405238ra/789147.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I liked <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/533510730" rel="nofollow noopener">Beauty from Pain</a>, even with the epic cliffy **shaking head**, so you can see how very excited I was for <i>Beauty from Surrender</i><br><br><b>Disclaimer</b> There is no cliffy in <i>Beauty from Surrender</i> and there’s a HEA, but there’s enough of an opening for book 3, which from reading Georgia Cate’s blog, hasn’t been decided if it’s going to be a full novel or novella. <br><br>I’ll tell you now… I will read book 3 and I prefer novels :D<br><br>We pick right where we left off from <i>Beauty from Pain</i> (if you haven’t read book 1, then stop reading) so Laurelyn went back to the states and Jack **gasp** wakes up with no Laurelyn. <br><br><b>Let’s be honest people, this is the sh!t I crave. Yeah!</b> <br>Stupid Jack Henry, why didn’t you tell Laurelyn you loved her?!<br><br><b>
  <i>I want her for-f&amp;cking-ever.</i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>I knew you were the next one the second I laid eyes on you singing in that club, but you can never imagine my surprise when I realized that you weren’t just the next one- you were the last one</i>
</b><br><br>You want her Jack Henry? Well do something about it! And he does. Laurelyn is depressed in the states, but she continues to pursue her singing career and at the same time Jack Henry tries to find her. This isn’t dragged out that long and I liked seeing Laruelyn in the states doing her own thing. It was different for me.<br><br><b>
  <i>There’s been no other mans since you- not inside my head, my heart or my body.</i>
</b><br><br>So, let’s address the very obvious thing I noticed. I would say about …. maybe more than half of the read is STEAM. Now, ladies, I’m all for those reads and honestly it didn’t take away from the read, but LORD… you will be fanning yourself. I only wish (mild complaint) it was kinkier! BUT that’s just me.<br><br><b>
  <i>I’m so pissed off right now that I can’t see straight. I simultaneously love the f&amp;ck out of you while I hate your guts. I don’t know if I want to slap your face or get naked with you.</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/ljiEQdZ" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380405238ra/789149.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>I don’t regret you for a second. You’re my favorite complication and you always will be.</i>
</b><br><br>Overall the tone and feel of the <i>Beauty from surrender</i> is VERY lovey and light, there is some tension and you can tell by my status updates when it happens.<br><br><b>At 15% … I’m happy<br><br>At 30%, it’s steamy, but I’m pretty happy<br><br>At 51% … yup more steamy scenes<br><br>At 86% there’s full blown out tension and I’m about to throw my tablet at the wall</b><br><br>At some parts, I wanted to punch Laurelyn in the face, BUT thank god for Addison, who kind of tries to be the voice of reason. Oh and my favorite scene… the one in the rain. I pictured that in my head, but instead of Laurelyn, I pictured myself. (Don’t act like you don’t do it too)<br><br>I liked <i>Beauty from Surrender</i>, steam and all, but what I enjoyed most was that I finally got the explanation of the title. I ALWAYS look for this in a read and yup, had a smile on my face when I got it.<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/WMOP66Y" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410173i/803851.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I think if you started the series, it would be good to finish it with <i>Beauty from Surrender</i> and from there you can decide if you want to move forward with book 3.<br><br><b>Series Order</b><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17156015.Beauty_from_Pain__Beauty___1_" title="Beauty from Pain (Beauty, #1) by Georgia Cates" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1360699932s/17156015.jpg" alt="Beauty from Pain (Beauty, #1) by Georgia Cates" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/533510730" rel="nofollow noopener">REVIEW</a> | <a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/148234873X/ref=as_li_qf_sp_asin_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=211189&amp;creative=373489&amp;creativeASIN=148234873X&amp;link_code=as3&amp;tag=jacqsread-20" rel="nofollow noopener">AMAZON</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17314410.Beauty_from_Surrender__Beauty___2_" title="Beauty from Surrender (Beauty, #2) by Georgia Cates" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_545824117" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/545824117" />
    <a title="April Avelino" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10703606-april-avelino"><img alt="April Avelino" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1391085470p2/10703606.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/545824117?book_show_action=true">Feb 25, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="April Avelino" class="user" itemprop="url" name="April Avelino" href="/user/show/10703606-april-avelino">April Avelino</a>
      </span>

          marked it as to-read




        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10703606-april-avelino?shelf=top-tbr">top-tbr</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('3HUK3Jg6f/6CmaPgcOGRWyqVlOX/as4ajlpM8yUsXG0JzTQMmhBxwKCXA6+NhQ5qQnMHq8JOoXOogmeU2z22gw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }
